DROP TABLE IF EXISTS video_games.dbo.game;

CREATE TABLE video_games.dbo.game (
	id INT PRIMARY KEY,
	genre_id INT,
	game_name VARCHAR(200),
	CONSTRAINT fk_gm_gen FOREIGN KEY (genre_id) REFERENCES video_games.dbo.genre(id)
);
